					String Quartet in E-flat major, Hob.III:38 (Haydn, Joseph)				</h1>

<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">String Quartet in E-flat major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">String Quartet No.38&#160;; "Russian Quartet No.2, The Joke"
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Haydn,_Joseph" title="Category:Haydn, Joseph">Haydn, Joseph</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/JosephHaydnThematisch-bibliographischesWerkverzeichnis/Hoboken1-3#page/n417/mode/2up">Hob.III:38</a></span>&#160;; Op.33 No.2
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJH 446
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>E-flat major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 movements:
<ol><li>Allegro moderato (E-flat major)
</li><li>Scherzando. Allegro - Trio (E-flat major)
</li><li>Largo sostenuto (B-flat major)
</li><li>Finale. Presto (E-flat major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1781
</td></tr>

<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication

<td>Russian Grand Duke Paul

</th>

</td></tr>
